### [77] [UniFormer: Efficient and Unified Model-Centric Scaling for Industrial Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27058)
*Bo Chen,Jinlong Jiao,Tijian Hu,Ruihao Zhang,Yanzhi Liu,Chenghou Jin,Qinglin Jia,Baixuan He,Hechang Pan,Yiwu Liu,Jian Liang,Chaoyi Ma,Ruiming Tang,Han Li,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: UniFormer 提出了一种统一的、以模型为中心的缩放框架，通过空间解耦和语义标记化实现了工业级推荐系统的高效建模与在线推理加速，并在大规模生产环境中取得了显著的业务提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推荐模型缩放方法大多局限于独立的组件缩放（如行为、特征或任务建模），或仅在特征空间内进行有限的跨模块联合缩放，缺乏统一的以模型为中心的缩放框架来全面提升大规模工业推荐系统的性能和效率。

Method: 1. 架构分解：将建模空间拆分为特征空间交互模块和任务空间交互模块；2. 推理加速：引入基于语义的标记化方案实现用户-物品解耦；3. 模式捕获：利用多序列交叉注意力捕获异构行为模式，结合自注意力增强交互建模；4. 弹性缩放：采用多视图前馈网络（FFN）支持不同组件间的灵活参数缩放。

Result: 在快手和快手极速版两个真实生产环境的在线 A/B 测试中，UniFormer 显著提升了用户互动指标，其中 App 使用时长分别提升了 +0.101% 和 +0.260%，观看时长分别提升了 +0.729% 和 +1.113%。

Conclusion: UniFormer 证明了通过统一的以模型为中心的缩放框架，能够打破传统组件级缩放的局限。该方法在工业级推荐系统中不仅提升了模型性能，还通过创新的语义标记化实现了高效的在线推理，为大规模推荐模型的设计提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Recently, substantial progress has been made in industrial recommendation through component-centric model scaling, where individual components such as behavior modeling, feature interaction, or task modeling are independently scaled to improve model capacity. Although recent methods such as HyFormer and OneTrans further explore cross-module co-scaling by jointly modeling behavior and interaction, their designs are still confined to the feature space and lack a unified model-centric scaling framework over the overall modeling space. In this paper, we propose UniFormer, an efficient and unified model-centric scaling framework for industrial recommender systems. To improve efficiency, UniFormer decomposes the overall modeling space into feature and task spaces, which are modeled by stacked Feature-space Interaction Modules and Task-space Interaction Modules, respectively. Moreover, UniFormer introduces semantic-based tokenization scheme to enable user-item decoupling, thereby achieving request-level inference acceleration. To prevent preference collapse, UniFormer employs multi-sequence cross-attention to separately capture heterogeneous behavior patterns, followed by the self-attention to enhance interaction modeling. Besides, dedicated multi-view FFNs are introduced to support flexible and scalable parameter scaling across different modeling components. Extensive online A/B testing in two production scenarios, Kuaishou and Kuaishou Lite, shows that UniFormer consistently improves user engagement and interaction metrics, achieving gains of +0.101%/+0.260% in App Stay Time and +0.729%/+1.113% in Watch Time, respectively.

</details>


### [78] [TRUST: Item-Calibrated Interval Evidence for Temporal Session-Based Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27214)
*Linjiang Guo,Nitin Bisht,Shiqing Wu,Yifan Yin,Guandong Xu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对现有会话推荐中直接使用绝对时间间隔导致语义偏差的问题，本文提出了TRUST框架。该框架通过考虑每个物品特定的时间间隔分布，对时间信号进行标准化校准，从而更精准地捕捉用户兴趣，在多个任务中均实现了性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间感知会话推荐模型大多直接使用绝对时间间隔，默认不同物品的时间间隔具有相同的语义。然而，作者通过实证发现不同物品具有各自独特的时间间隔分布，因此绝对间隔无法准确反映真实的用户兴趣，需要根据物品特性对时间间隔进行校准。

Method: 提出了TRUST框架，核心在于引入了一个基于物品经验分布的评分函数，对时间间隔进行校准。具体包括：1. 基于校准后的评分进行全局邻居采样；2. 在会话图编码中融合校准的时间信息；3. 在兴趣聚合阶段利用评分函数优化特征加权。该方法不仅作为独立模型使用，还可作为插件增强现有的时间感知会话推荐模型。

Result: 在多个公开数据集上的实验证明，TRUST在推荐性能上始终优于主流的时间感知及非时间感知基准模型；插件实验表明，所提评分函数能有效提升现有会话推荐模型的效果，消融实验证实了在不同模块中进行时间校准均能带来一致的性能改进。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在会话推荐中将时间间隔进行“物品级”标准化处理（而非使用绝对值）是捕捉用户兴趣的关键，TRUST框架通过这种校准机制能够显著提升推荐性能，并具有良好的通用性和可移植性。

Abstract: Temporal signals have been widely used in session-based recommendation to infer user interest. Existing temporal session-based recommenders primarily rely on absolute interval values, implicitly assuming that the same interval carries similar interest signals across items. However, we empirically find that this assumption does not hold: each item has its own interval distribution, so an interval should be interpreted relative to the item it belongs to. Based on this observation, we propose TRUST, a framework that evaluates each observed interval relative to the empirical interval distribution of the corresponding item. Specifically, we propose a score function to guide global neighbor sampling, session graph encoding, and final interest aggregation. Experiments on public datasets show that TRUST consistently improves over representative temporal and non-temporal baselines, and plug-in experiments further show that the proposed scoring function can improve existing temporal session recommenders as a model-agnostic method. Component-wise ablations further show that calibrating the temporal signals within each module, rather than removing the module itself, consistently improves neighbor sampling, session graph encoding, and interest aggregation.

</details>


### [79] [NOVA: A Verification-Aware Agent Harness for Architecture Evolution in Industrial Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27243)
*Shaohua Liu,Liang Fang,Yilong Sun,Shudong Huang,Qingsong Luo,Xiaoyang Chen,Dongqiang Liu,Chuangang Ma,Zhenzhen Chai,Henghuan Wang,Shijie Quan,Changyuan Cui,Zhangbin Zhu,Peng Chen,Wei Xu,Lei Xiao,Haijie Gu,Jie Jiang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了 NOVA，一个针对推荐系统模型架构演进的验证感知型智能体框架。它通过架构梯度引导演进、多级验证机制屏蔽无效方案，以及分级人机协作模式，成功在工业生产中实现了高效且稳健的模型架构升级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业广告推荐系统的模型架构演进依赖于专家经验，不仅耗时且难以规模化。现有的 AutoML 主要局限于超参数调优，而通用的 LLM 编码智能体缺乏对推荐系统领域语义的深刻理解，容易产生导致性能下降的“沉默故障”（Silent Failures）。

Method: 提出了一种名为 NOVA 的智能体框架：1. 使用“架构梯度”（Architecture Gradient），一种模拟 SGD 的非微分更新信号来引导架构修改；2. 实施“验证级联”（Verification Cascade），在多个维度对架构进行严格检查，并在失败时记录“禁止方向”；3. 采用“L1-L4 任务级控制”，根据任务风险和复杂度决定自动化程度，确保高风险任务有人工参与。

Result: NOVA 在 L2 和 L3 任务上实现了 54.5% 和 60.0% 的最高有效通过率，显著降低了沉默故障率；将从文献到生产的周期缩短了 13 倍以上；在线 A/B 测试中，GMV 提升最高达 2.02%，同时显著降低了预测偏差。

Conclusion: NOVA 证明了通过结合架构梯度、验证级联和分级控制，可以实现工业级推荐模型架构的自动化演进，不仅显著提升了研发效率，还保证了模型在复杂生产环境下的性能稳健性。

Abstract: Industrial advertising recommender models are continuously improved through architecture evolution. Upgrades such as RankMixer, TokenMixer-Large, and MixFormer show that better structures remain a key source of quality and business gains. Yet developing such upgrades in production is expert-intensive and difficult to scale. Existing automation is insufficient: AutoML mainly tunes hyper-parameters, while effective gains often require cross-module changes under strict constraints; generic LLM coding agents optimize for runnable code, but runnable code does not imply a valid recommender architecture. Candidates may pass local tests while causing silent failures that degrade performance.
  We present NOVA, a level-aware agent harness for verification-aware architecture evolution. NOVA uses an architecture gradient, an SGD-inspired, non-differentiable update signal that aggregates prior modifications, verification diagnostics, metric feedback, and trajectory memory to guide the next modification. A verification cascade checks structure semantics, local executability, offline effectiveness, and online impact; invalid candidates are blocked early, with failure patterns recorded as forbidden directions. L1--L4 task-level control matches automation to task complexity and risk, routing high-risk tasks to Copilot for human oversight. Deployed in an industrial advertising system, NOVA achieves the highest effective pass rate on L2 ScaleUp and L3 Literature-to-Production tasks (54.5% and 60.0%), reduces silent failures compared with coding-agent baselines, and shortens one literature-to-production cycle by over 13x in human-attended time. In online A/B testing, the selected L3 candidate improves GMV on three pCVR objectives by +1.25%, +1.70%, and +2.02%, while reducing pCVR bias by 58.8%, 66.7%, and 37.3%.

</details>

### [80] [Physics-guided Convolutional Neural Network for Domain Growth Prediction in Systems with Conserved Kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26128)
*Vijay Yadav,Madhu Priya,Manish Dev Shrimali,Prabhat K. Jaiswal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于注意力机制的物理引导卷积神经网络，用于高效模拟Cahn-Hilliard方程驱动的复杂相分离过程。该模型在保持物理守恒规律的同时，实现了对系统长时间演化的精准预测，且符合经典的物理生长定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解器在模拟复杂的非线性偏微分方程（PDE）时计算成本高昂。随着深度学习的发展，基于深度神经网络的替代模型（Surrogate Models）成为解决这一问题的热门研究方向，旨在通过数据驱动与物理约束相结合的方式，实现对物理、化学及生物系统时空演化的高效、精准模拟。

Method: 提出了一种结合注意力机制与物理引导（Physics-guided）的卷积神经网络架构。该模型通过将物理方程的约束融入深度学习框架中，专门用于学习和预测描述微观结构演化（如Cahn-Hilliard方程支配的二元混合物相分离）的非线性偏微分方程。模型通过训练实现对相分离过程全时间演化的精确预测。

Result: 实验结果表明，该替代模型在长时滚动预测中保持了极高的稳定性和准确性，适用于临界和非临界混合物。模型不仅成功保持了混合物成分的守恒，还准确刻画了结构域尺寸的增长，并与经典的Lifshitz-Slyozov领域生长定律高度一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于注意力机制的物理引导卷积神经网络模型，能够高效且准确地模拟具有守恒动力学的复杂系统（如Cahn-Hilliard方程描述的相分离过程）。该框架在长时预测、保持守恒律以及捕捉宏观物理规律（如Lifshitz-Slyozov生长律）方面表现优异，证明了其作为传统数值求解器高效替代方案的潜力，并具有扩展至其他复杂动力学系统的广泛前景。

Abstract: The spatiotemporal evolution of many physical, chemical, and biological systems is described by nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs). Recently, deep neural network-based surrogate models have gained increasing interest as efficient alternatives to computationally expensive traditional numerical solvers. In this work, we propose an attention-based, physics-guided convolutional neural network as a surrogate model to learn the microstructural evolution of such systems. We train the model to accurately predict the full time-evolution of phase separation in binary mixtures governed by the Cahn-Hilliard equation. We show that predictions from our trained surrogate model remain stable and accurate over long-time rollouts for both critical and off-critical mixtures and preserve the mixture composition throughout evolution. We also show that our model accurately captures the growth of domain size and is consistent with the Lifshitz-Slyozov domain-growth law. The prediction results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework for modeling systems with conserved kinetics and can be extended to other complex dynamical systems.

### [81] [\chisao{}: A GPU-Native Parallel Optimizer for Multimodal Black-Box Functions via Convergence-Anticonvergence Oscillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26164)
*Ira Wolfson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CHISAO 是一款基于 GPU 的新型黑盒多模态优化算法，通过独特的振荡循环机制，在保持极高模态恢复率的同时，实现了相比传统串行算法数十倍的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态黑盒函数优化方法（如 basin-hopping、CMA-ES 等）多为串行执行，无法充分利用现代 GPU 的大规模并行计算能力，且在高维环境下极易陷入局部最优，难以高效恢复所有模态。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CHISAO 的 GPU 原生群体优化器，核心机制包括“收敛-反收敛”振荡循环（用于跳出局部陷阱）、模态冻结策略（锁定已发现的峰值）、基于动量的反收敛探索以及两种互补的自适应重播种策略（Repulse Monkey 和 Golden Rooster）来维持种群多样性。该方法完全基于导数无关的有限差分，适用于黑盒函数。

Result: 在包含 42 个函数的 SFU 基准测试集上（维度高达 64D），CHISAO 实现了 100% 的模态恢复率，而在相同条件下传统 CPU 基准测试方法多在 8D 以上失效；相较于 basin-hopping，CHISAO 在多模态函数上实现了高达 34 倍的加速，在单模态函数上更是达到了 39 倍的加速，且在强噪声环境下依然保持高度可靠。

Conclusion: CHISAO 通过独特的振荡循环机制和 GPU 并行优化，解决了传统优化算法在处理高维多模态黑盒函数时易陷入局部最优及效率低下的问题，验证了其在高维空间和存在噪声环境下的极高鲁棒性与性能优势。

Abstract: Finding all modes of a multimodal black-box function is a fundamental challenge in optimization, Bayesian inference, and scientific computing. Existing approaches -- basin-hopping, CMA-ES, multistart gradient descent -- operate sequentially and cannot exploit the massive parallelism of modern GPU hardware. We introduce \chisao{} (\textbf{C}onvergence-\textbf{H}alt-\textbf{I}nvert-\textbf{S}tick-\textbf{A}nd-\textbf{O}scillate), a GPU-native population optimizer that runs an entire sample batch simultaneously and exploits a deliberate convergence-anticonvergence oscillation cycle to escape local traps while freezing confirmed modes. The structural move is asymmetric: samples that reach true peaks are frozen (``stuck'') and preserved, while the rest keep exploring via momentum-based anti-convergence and stochastically smoothed gradients. Adaptive reseeding via two complementary strategies (Repulse Monkey and Golden Rooster) maintains population diversity throughout. On all 42 functions of the Simon Fraser University optimization benchmark suite across dimensions $d \in \{2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64\}$, \chisao{} achieves \textbf{100\%} mode recovery where all CPU baselines collapse at $d \geq 8$ on the hardest multimodal functions, at up to \textbf{$34\times$} speedup over basin-hopping on functions where all methods succeed (Michalewicz $d=64$) and up to \textbf{$39\times$} on unimodal functions (Rotated Hyper-Ellipsoid $d=64$, pure GPU dividend). All benchmarks evaluate the objective by value alone -- gradients come from finite differences -- so the reported speedups are a derivative-free worst case. Under substantial likelihood noise ($σ_{\mathrm{noise}}$ up to 1.0), mode detection remains 100\% reliable. The algorithm is available as a standalone open-source Python package on PyPI.

</details>


### [82] [Implementation of reinforcement learning in chemical reaction networks: application to phototaxis as curiosity-driven exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26168)
*Ruyi Tang,Grégoire Sergeant-Perthuis,David Colliaux*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合POMDP与生化反应网络的模型，解释了单细胞生物如何将“奔跑-翻滚”的行为作为一种主动降低环境感知不确定性的策略，从微观生化机制层面揭示了细胞的“最小认知”导航原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单细胞趋光性模型多将其视为简单的刺激-反应过程，忽略了生物体如何通过主动采样环境来减少感官歧义。研究旨在从“最小认知”（minimal cognition）的角度，探讨单细胞生物如何利用生化网络实现信息驱动的传感器运动策略。

Method: 1. 理论建模：利用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）框架结合生化反应动力学（CRN-ODEs）来描述细胞行为。
2. 贝叶斯推断：通过无记忆贝叶斯更新过程处理隐藏的环境变量，平衡定向与探索。
3. 实验验证与计算：利用逆向强化学习（IRL）对30条衣藻（Chlamydomonas）轨迹进行分析，反推出行为目标函数，并与随机模拟算法（SSA）进行对比评估。

Result: 研究表明该模型能够有效复现衣藻的实验性趋光轨迹，其效果与标准的SSA基准相当。实验结果证实了“翻滚”行为在功能上起到重定向作用，即通过采样新的感官配置来优化对环境信息的感知，实现了适应性的信息获取。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了单细胞生物的趋光性不仅是机械性的反应，更是一种主动的信息获取过程。通过将细胞行为建模为POMDP，证明了“奔跑-翻滚”（run-tumble）机制本质上是细胞为了降低感知模糊度而采取的策略，且这种复杂的行为能够通过细胞内的生化反应网络（CRN）实现。

Abstract: Living systems navigate environments using noisy and incomplete sensory signals. In unicellular algae, phototaxis is often modeled as a mechanistic run--tumble process driven by stimulus--response rules. However, such descriptions overlook how organisms actively sample their environment to reduce sensory ambiguity. From a minimal cognition perspective, we reframe this navigation as a subjective, information-driven sensorimotor process. To this end, we propose a framework linking a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) with biochemical reaction dynamics. Environmental variables are hidden, while the cell updates a minimal internal state from each observation through a memoryless Bayesian step. These internal dynamics balance orienting toward light with exploratory reorientation and can be implemented through Chemical-Reaction-Network Ordinary Differential Equations (CRN--ODEs). Our model includes a biophysical observation process for photoreception and a chemically computable polynomial bound on information gain. Using Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) on 30 experimentally recorded Chlamydomonas trajectories, we infer the behavioral objective consistent with observed phototactic motion and benchmark the resulting dynamics with standard Stochastic Simulation Algorithm (SSA) baselines. Our model reproduces the empirical alignment-to-light distribution, comparable to objective SSA baselines on this dataset. Within this framework, run--tumble alternation emerges as an information-acquisition strategy: tumbling reorients the cell to sample new sensory configurations and resolve sensor ambiguity, demonstrating how intracellular biochemical networks can support adaptive information-seeking behavior in cellular navigation.

</details>


### [83] [Neural Architecture Search for Generative Adversarial Networks: A Comprehensive Review and Critical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26169)
*Abrar Alotaibi,Moataz Ahmed*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成对抗网络（GAN）的架构设计复杂且依赖人工经验，具有一定的挑战性。NAS作为一种自动化设计技术，旨在解决手动设计架构的局限性，从而优化GAN的整体性能。

Method: 本文对现有的神经架构搜索（NAS）应用于生成对抗网络（GAN）的方法进行了系统性综述。通过梳理和归纳，作者依据搜索策略（如进化算法、基于梯度的方法）、评估指标以及性能表现对各类研究进行了分类、对比和分析。

Result: 研究发现，进化算法和基于梯度的NAS方法在不同应用场景下各具优势。此外，该分析指出传统评估指标（IS、FID）存在局限性，强调了开发更稳健的评估标准以及使用多样化数据集进行测试的必要性。

Conclusion: 神经网络架构搜索（NAS）能够显著提升生成对抗网络（GAN）的性能、稳定性和效率。该领域未来的发展方向应聚焦于超越传统评估指标（如IS和FID）的鲁棒性评估方法，以及在更多样化的数据集上验证算法的泛化能力。

Abstract: Neural Architecture Search (NAS) has emerged as a pivotal technique in optimizing the design of Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs), automating the search for effective architectures while addressing the challenges inherent in manual design. This paper provides a comprehensive review of NAS methods applied to GANs, categorizing and comparing various approaches based on criteria such as search strategies, evaluation metrics, and performance outcomes. The review highlights the benefits of NAS in improving GAN performance, stability, and efficiency, while also identifying limitations and areas for future research. Key findings include the superiority of evolutionary algorithms and gradient-based methods in certain contexts, the importance of robust evaluation metrics beyond traditional scores like Inception Score (IS) and Fréchet Inception Distance (FID), and the need for diverse datasets in assessing GAN performance. By presenting a structured comparison of existing NAS-GAN techniques, this paper aims to guide researchers in developing more effective NAS methods and advancing the field of GANs.

### [84] [KG-TRACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Mechanistic Grounding in Antimicrobial Resistance Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26179)
*Naman Garg,Sarika Jain,Sourav Yadav,Bharat K. Bhargava,Ghanapriya Singh,Abhishek Srivastava,Parimal Kar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KG-TRACE 是一种将世界卫生组织（WHO）知识图谱与深度学习相结合的神经符号模型，旨在解决 AMR 预测模型缺乏临床可解释性的问题，实现了高性能预测与生物学证据的深度结合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于 WGS 的 AMR 预测模型虽然准确度较高，但缺乏将神经预测归因与已知生物通路联系起来的机制，导致模型表现为“黑盒”，难以在临床环境中建立信任。

Method: 提出了一种名为 KG-TRACE 的神经符号框架。该方法结合了基于神经网络的基因组分析与 WHO 突变知识图谱（KG）。通过 RotatE 算法生成 KG 嵌入，利用“认识论信任门”（epistemic trust gate）动态平衡深度学习特征与符号化生物知识，并引入“生物学接地比率”（BGR）指标来衡量模型归因与已知生物学的一致性。

Result: 在 CRyPTIC 结核分枝杆菌队列中，该模型针对异烟肼的预测 AUC 达到 0.9760，实现了 92.5% 的符号覆盖率。此外，该模型能有效识别多重耐药性（MDR）共现伪影，并为临床提供可验证的审计追踪。

Conclusion: 本研究通过神经符号学习方法成功将生物学知识纳入全基因组测序（WGS）抗微生物药物耐药性（AMR）预测模型中。KG-TRACE 不仅实现了高准确率，更重要的是提供了一个可解释、可审计的临床决策支持框架，显著提升了模型的可信度和临床实用性。

Abstract: While WGS-based AMR prediction has reached high accuracy, existing models lack a mechanism to ground neural attributions in established biological pathways. We present KG-TRACE, a novel neuro-symbolic framework that integrates the WHO mutation knowledge graph (KG) as a structured biological constraint on a neural genomic model. Unlike existing methods that learn statistical patterns in isolation, KG-TRACE fuses genomic features and RotatE-based KG embeddings through a learned epistemic trust gate, dynamically weighting neural evidence against symbolic biological knowledge.
  Evaluated on the CRyPTIC M. tuberculosis cohort, KG-TRACE achieves an AUROC of 0.9760 for isoniazid, achieving competitive accuracy while its primary value lies in symbolic grounding, not predictive uplift. More importantly, we introduce the Biological Grounding Ratio (BGR), a dataset-level metric that quantifies alignment between neural attributions and established biology. Our framework achieves a 92.5% symbolic coverage of isoniazid-resistant predictions and effectively identifies MDR co-occurrence artifacts by issuing laboratory follow-up flags for 'UNCERTAIN' cases. We demonstrate that neuro-symbolic grounding provides a verifiable audit trail for clinicians, bridging the gap between predictive accuracy and clinical trust.

</details>


### [85] [Necessary but Not Sufficient: Temperature Control and Reproducibility in LLM-as-Judge Safety Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26185)
*Hiroki Tamba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了大模型作为安全评估器时，普遍被认为“设定温度为0即可确定”的假设是错误的。即便强制贪婪采样，评估结果仍存在显著噪声，因此必须引入对评估器分歧度的监测，而非仅依赖单次评估结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前业界普遍认为将大模型评估器（LLM-as-judge）的采样温度设为0即可保证评估结果的确定性。研究者质疑这一假设，旨在揭示现有评估工具包在安全决策时因不可重复性导致的噪声问题。

Method: 研究人员针对日本AISI的开源安全评估代码库（aisev）进行了实证测试，分析了不同模型层级、不同API提供商以及不同采样配置（包括默认温度和强制贪婪解码）下的评估一致性，并对690次API调用进行了重复性实验。

Result: 1. 默认设置下，评估器在没有显式设置温度时会使用默认值1.0，导致判定结果在多次运行中存在极高不确定性（单项差异高达50%）；2. 即使强制设定温度为0或使用贪婪解码，仍有部分临界样本无法保证结果的一致性；3. 新型模型已逐渐弃用温度参数，使得既有的缓解方案失效。

Conclusion: “大模型作为裁判”的评估方法存在显著的不可重复性，即使在温度设为0的情况下也无法完全消除噪声。评估工具包不应仅报告单次运行的通过/失败结果，而应将“裁判分歧度”作为评估安全性的关键指标。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge ("grader") components are now standard in evaluation harnesses, including safety evaluations where a pass/fail verdict may gate downstream deployment decisions. A widespread assumption is that setting the grader's sampling temperature to 0 makes grading deterministic. We test this assumption against a real safety-evaluation codebase (Japan AISI's open-source aisev) and show it fails on two levels. First, the harness invokes its grader without setting temperature or seed; the underlying provider silently applies its default of 1.0, so items near the decision boundary flip pass/fail across identical runs (per-item disagreement up to ~50% over 20 runs). Second, pinning temperature=0 reduces but does not eliminate flips: across 690 API calls spanning two providers, three model tiers, and five sampling configurations, 1-2 of 7 borderline items remain non-reproducible even under forced greedy decoding (top_k=1). Claude Opus 4.7/4.8 has since deprecated temperature entirely, rendering the primary mitigation inapplicable to newer model generations. These findings expose a structural gap: evaluation harnesses that report single-run verdicts without variance or grader-disagreement metrics can present noise as a safety property. We release a reproduction harness (690 calls, 7 conditions) and recommend that harnesses treat grader disagreement as a first-class health metric alongside the scores themselves.

</details>


### [86] [Clue-Guided Money Laundering Group Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26189)
*Boyang Wang,Jianing Cao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 Clue2Group 的框架：首先，构建紧凑的局部调查上下文以过滤噪声并保留洗钱特征结构；其次，利用多语义局部时间图神经网络（GNN）估计线索条件下的局部风险场；最后，融合风险、结构和先验模式证据，逐步恢复完整的洗钱团伙结构。

Result: 在两个大规模反洗钱基准测试上的实验结果表明，Clue2Group 能够有效地实现线索驱动的团伙发现，在恢复洗钱团伙结构方面表现出色，并成功缩短了图计算研究与实际调查工作流之间的差距。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 Clue2Group 框架成功将图论异常检测与现实的反洗钱调查流程相结合，证明了基于线索的循序渐进式发现方法在处理大规模金融网络洗钱团伙时的有效性和实用性，为反洗钱研究提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Money Laundering Group Discovery (MLGD) aims to identify hidden criminal groups and recover their complete structures in large-scale financial networks. Existing graph anomaly detection methods mainly produce node-level risk alerts, while global group discovery methods passively search for suspicious groups over the whole network. Both are mismatched with real Anti-money-laundering (AML) investigations, where analysts usually start from a concrete clue and gradually expand the investigation to recover the responsible group. To address this gap, we propose Clue-Guided Group Discovery (CGGD), where a laundering group is progressively recovered from an initial clue set through analyst interaction. We further propose Clue2Group, a framework that first constructs a compact local investigation context to reduce noise and preserve chain-like and cycle-like laundering structures. It then estimates a clue-conditioned local risk field with a multi-semantic local-temporal GNN, and finally integrates risk, structural, and prior-pattern evidence to recover a coherent laundering group. Experiments on two large-scale AML benchmarks show that Clue2Group provides a practical clue-driven analysis framework for AML investigations, offering a feasible step toward bridging the gap between graph-based AML research and real investigation workflows.

### [87] [Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26192)
*Jialan He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 FHPLF 的联邦哈希投影潜在因子模型，通过引入二值梯度优化、投影汉明距离相似度建模及安全隐私增强上传策略，有效解决了联邦哈希学习中存在的通信开销大、隐私风险高以及二值编码表示能力不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统哈希学习需集中数据导致隐私风险；现有联邦学习依赖传输大规模实值梯度，导致通信开销大且存在隐私隐患；现有哈希联邦学习方法受限于二值码的有限表达能力，导致模型精度下降。

Method: 1. 提出使用二值梯度类矩阵替代实数值梯度矩阵，降低计算、存储与通信负担；2. 采用投影汉明距离（Projected Hamming Distance）进行相似度建模，提升二值码的表示能力；3. 设计安全二值梯度重组与隐私增强上传（SBG-PEU）策略，进一步降低用户交互泄露风险。

Result: 在四个真实数据集上的实验结果表明，FHPLF 模型在准确性、效率和隐私保护方面均优于现有的先进哈希学习与联邦学习方法。

Conclusion: FHPLF 模型有效地整合了哈希学习与联邦学习的优势，在保证高隐私性和低通信开销的同时，克服了传统二值编码表示能力受限的问题，实现了模型精度、效率与隐私保护之间的良好平衡。

Abstract: Hash Learning (HL) is an efficient representation learning approach that maps real-valued data into compact binary representations. Traditional HL methods typically require users to upload personal data to a central server, which is incompatible with increasingly stringent data security regulations. Federated Learning (FL) provides a decentralized paradigm for learning globally optimal models without centralizing private data. However, most FL methods rely on transmitting large-scale real-valued gradient information, leading to high communication overhead and potential privacy risks. Integrating HL into FL is a promising solution. Nevertheless, existing HL methods suffer from limited representational capacity of binary codes, which may degrade model accuracy. To address this challenge, we propose a Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor (FHPLF) model. FHPLF introduces three key innovations: (a) replacing real-valued gradient matrices with binary gradient-like matrices, significantly reducing computation, storage, and communication costs while enhancing privacy protection; (b) leveraging Projected Hamming Distance for similarity modeling, which captures the importance of individual binary bits to improve representation capability; and (c) proposing a Secure Binary Gradient Reassembly and Privacy-Enhanced Upload (SBG-PEU) strategy to further reduce the risk of user interaction leakage during transmission. Extensive experiments on four real-world datasets demonstrate that FHPLF consistently outperforms state-of-the-art HL and FL methods, achieving a favorable trade-off among accuracy, efficiency, and privacy preservation.

Method: 本研究指出并批判了当前算法公平性研究中的两大核心局限：一是审计过程中对确定性点估计（deterministic point estimates）的过度依赖；二是将个体视为脱离结构性社会背景的孤立实体进行处理的简化做法。研究旨在通过克服这些局限，提出更具适应性和深度的公平性分析框架。

Conclusion: 算法公平性研究需要超越单纯的数学建模，必须将社会技术背景、结构性不平等以及不确定性纳入评估框架，才能从根本上解决算法偏见问题。

Abstract: Modern machine learning systems have outgrown their origins as isolated predictive constructs, evolving into complex socio-technical architectures that actively mediate human opportunity. As algorithms increasingly determine access to economic and social opportunities, it has become widely recognized that these systems are deeply embedded with the structural inequalities and prejudices of their environments. The field of algorithmic fairness emerged in response to the growing recognition that models optimized for predictive accuracy can systematically disadvantage marginalized groups. Early mitigation strategies, however, rested on fragile simplifications that limited their effectiveness in complex socio-technical environments. This thesis identifies and addresses two fundamental limitations of contemporary fairness paradigms: the reliance on deterministic point estimates for auditing and the treatment of individuals as isolated entities devoid of structural context.

### [91] [Fast LeWorldModel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26217)
*Yuntian Gao,Xiangyu Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LeWorldModel 在视觉规划中依赖逐步的自回归展开，导致计算开销大，且随着预测时间跨度的增加，潜空间内的误差累积效应严重。

Method: 提出 Fast-LeWM，将传统的逐步自回归预测改进为基于动作前缀的并行预测；该方法直接将动作序列前缀作为预测单元，通过一次性并行预测多个时间步的潜在状态，而非反复迭代计算。

Result: 在多项任务中，Fast-LeWM 不仅显著降低了规划耗时，还在开放环路潜空间损失评估中表现更优，有效抑制了长序列预测中的误差增长，提升了规划成功率。

Abstract: Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs), including recent LeWorldModel (LeWM), have become a promising foundation for reconstruction-free visual world models. For visual planning, however, LeWM evaluates candidate action sequences by repeatedly applying a local one-step latent transition model. This autoregressive rollout makes planning computationally expensive and exposes the predicted trajectory to accumulated latent errors as the horizon grows. We propose Fast LeWorldModel (Fast-LeWM), a fast latent world model that replaces repeated local rollout with action-prefix prediction. Given the current latent and a candidate action sequence, Fast-LeWM encodes its prefixes and predicts the future latents reached after executing those prefixes in parallel. By making action prefixes the basic prediction unit, Fast-LeWM directly models action effects accumulated to different extents over multiple horizons. This prefix-level supervision forces the model to learn how states continuously evolve under different action prefixes, rather than only fitting one-step state transitions. During planning, the predictor can use the last prefix token from the encoded action sequence to evaluate the corresponding future latent without explicitly rolling through each intermediate imagined state. Across multiple tasks, Fast-LeWM improves average success over LeWM while substantially reducing planning time, achieving lower open-loop latent loss whose growth becomes significantly slower as the rollout horizon increases.

### [92] [Dataset Usage Inference without Shadow Models or Held-out Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26257)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据集使用推理（DUI）方法存在局限性，通常需要训练昂贵的影子模型，且要求获取已知的训练样本和确实未参与训练的分布内数据集，这些条件在现代大规模模型和实际数据纠纷中难以满足，因此亟需一种更实用的DUI方法。

Method: 提出了一种无需影子模型和真实保留集（held-out set）的DUI框架。该方法通过生成合成的非成员样本（synthetic non-member samples）来构建参考基准，提取多维度的成员推断信号（membership signals），并将数据使用量估计问题转化为混合比例估计（mixture proportion estimation）问题。

Result: 在大型图像生成模型上的实验表明，该方法能够可靠地量化数据集的使用比例，即使在缺乏先验知识的实际应用场景下，也能准确评估特定数据集对模型训练的贡献。

Abstract: How much of my data was used to train a machine learning model? Dataset Usage Inference (DUI) aims to answer this by estimating what fraction of a dataset contributed to a model's training. However, existing DUI methods rely on assumptions that rarely hold in practice: they require training expensive shadow models to imitate the target model, and they assume access to both known training samples and an in-distribution held-out set confirmed to be absent from training. These conditions make current approaches impractical for modern large models and real data ownership disputes. We introduce a practical DUI framework that removes these constraints. Our method requires neither shadow models nor real held-out data. Instead, it generates synthetic non-member samples, extracts diverse membership signals, and casts DUI as a mixture proportion estimation problem to estimate what share of the candidate dataset was used during training. Experiments on large image generative models show that our method reliably quantifies dataset usage, providing a practical tool for data owners to determine how much of their data was used to train a model.

### [93] [Equivariance and Augmentation for Bayesian Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26273)
*Miaowen Dong,Axel Flinth,Jan E. Gerken*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度学习中，关于是通过架构设计强制实现等变性（等变神经网络），还是通过数据增强学习对称性，一直存在争议。尽管等变网络有较多理论研究，但数据增强的机制仍不清晰。本文旨在研究通过变分推理训练的贝叶斯神经网络中，数据增强如何实现等变性，从而更好地理解和优化这一过程。

Method: 该研究聚焦于采用变分推理训练的贝叶斯神经网络（BNNs），利用指数族变分分布推导了实现精确等变的条件；分析了数据增强对等变性的影响，并推导了等变性误差边界；提出了三种创新的对称化技术，包括轨道展开（orbit expansion）等，以增强数据增强的效果。

Result: 研究推导出了BNNs达到精确等变的数学条件，并给出了等变性误差的界限。数值实验证明，所提出的轨道展开方法在等变性和整体预测性能上均显著优于基准方法，验证了该方案在实际应用中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过在贝叶斯神经网络（BNNs）中引入特定的对称化技术，可以在不完全强制架构不变性的前提下，实现接近等变的性能。轨道展开（orbit expansion）方法被证明在提升等变性和模型表现方面最为有效，为在数据增强与架构设计之间进行权衡提供了理论依据和实用工具。

Abstract: Symmetries are important for many deep learning tasks, ranging from applications in the sciences to medical imaging. However, there is an ongoing debate about whether to impose symmetry constraints on the neural network architecture (yielding equivariant neural networks) or learn them from augmented training data. Although equivariant networks are well-studied theoretically, much less is known about data augmentation, since analyzing augmentation requires control over the training dynamics. Inspired by recent results that show that augmented infinite deep ensembles are exactly equivariant, we study data augmentation for Bayesian neural networks (BNNs) trained with variational inference. We focus on variational distributions in the exponential family and derive conditions under which exact equivariance is reached. We furthermore obtain bounds on the equivariance error and introduce three novel symmetrization techniques which boost the effect of data augmentation in this setting. We conduct extensive numerical experiments which show that one of our symmetrization methods (orbit expansion) outperforms the baseline in both equivariance and overall performance. Our code is available at github.com/dmw1998/augment-BNNs

</details>


### [94] [SSM Adapters via Hankel Reduced-order Modeling: Injection Site Determines Task Suitability in Long-Context Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26290)
*Omanshu Thapliyal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于状态空间模型（SSM）的参数高效微调适配器HRM，通过平衡截断与FFT加速，显著提升了大型语言模型在长上下文任务中的序列状态累积能力，性能超越了传统的LoRA方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Hankel降阶模型（HRM）”的适配器。该方法利用平衡截断（Balanced Truncation）技术初始化基于SSM的残差模块，并通过汉克尔算子（Hankel Grammians）实现对模型状态的降阶处理。同时，HRM利用系统矩阵的平移不变性，实现了基于FFT的高效并行扫描算法，确保了与LoRA相当的计算复杂度。

We introduce Hankel Reduced order Model (HRM) adapter, an SSM-based residual module initialized via Balanced Truncation of empirical Hankel Grammians. By leveraging the time-invariance of the system matrix $\bar{A}$, HRM enables an exact FFT-based parallel scan, achieving computational parity with LoRA across all context lengths. In iso-parametric evaluations on Mistral-7B (8.4M trainable parameters), HRM outperforms LoRA variants on LongBench tasks, including QuALITY (+34.8\% relative accuracy) and QMSum (+71.6\% relative ROUGE-1). HRM further demonstrates consistent superiority across 18 configurations of synthetic state-tracking (DFA, Parity) and character-level language modeling (enwik8). ### [95] [The Red Queen Gödel Machine: Co-Evolving Agents and Their Evaluators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26294)
*Alex Iacob,Andrej Jovanović,William F. Shen,Daniel Burkhardt,Meghdad Kurmanji,Nurbek Tastan,Lorenzo Sani,Niccolò Alberto Elia Venanzi,Ambroise Odonnat,Zeyu Cao,Bill Marino,Xinchi Qiu,Nicholas D. Lane*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有自我改进智能体受限于静态评估的问题，论文提出了“红皇后哥德尔机（RQGM）”，通过引入非平稳效用和演进式的评估机制，使智能体能够动态优化评估与执行，在代码生成及复杂的学术论文评审等任务中显著超越了现有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自我改进智能体多依赖于静态的评估准则（如固定的测试集或评分器），这忽略了智能体在进化过程中环境也在随之改变的现实。作者旨在通过引入演进的评估者、对抗性目标和动态效用函数，使评估机制成为自我改进循环的一部分，从而突破静态基准测试的局限。

Method: 提出了“红皇后哥德尔机”（RQGM），这是一种在非平稳效用下进行递归自我改进的进化框架。核心策略是将搜索过程分为多个周期，在周期内维持固定的评估准则，而在周期边界更新效用函数，从而在演进的评估环境下保证自我改进的有效性。该方法利用“智能体作为裁判”的机制，通过协同进化实现代码审查、科学论文评审及数学证明写作与评分的闭环优化。

Result: RQGM 在多种任务中表现优异：在代码任务中，以较少的 token 使用量超过了先前的 SOTA；在论文写作与评审任务中，协同进化的智能体获得了更高的录用率和 ground-truth 评分准确率；在对抗性评审实验中，成功修正了传统 AI 审稿人过度偏袒 AI 生成内容的偏差，达到了与人类审稿人相当的严格程度。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了引入动态、对抗性的评估机制可以显著提升智能体自我改进的效率和上限。通过在非平稳效用框架下协同进化，智能体不仅能克服静态基准测试的局限，还能在复杂任务中实现比传统方法更高的性能和更好的公平性。

Abstract: Self-improving agents are state-of-the-art (SOTA) on agentic coding benchmarks and have recently been extended to general domains. However, their search methods generally assume a stationary evaluation criterion: a fixed verifier, benchmark, or labeled dataset that remains valid as the agent improves. This ignores a central feature of evolution: species adapt as their environments change with them. We aim to bring the same principle to recursive self-improvement, making evaluation part of the improvement loop and opening search to evolving evaluators, adversarial objectives, and dynamic utilities that may surpass static benchmarks. We introduce the Red Queen Godel Machine (RQGM), an evolutionary framework for recursive self-improvement under non-stationary utilities. The RQGM makes this possible through controlled utility evolution: search is organized into epochs with a fixed within-epoch evaluation criterion, while the utility can be updated at epoch boundaries, so self-improvement guarantees hold per epoch as the objective evolves across them. We begin by showing that even on verifiable coding tasks, the RQGM improves test pass rate over the prior SOTA by adding a complementary agent-as-a-judge code-review signal. This signal is cheaper and the RQGM uses 1.35x-1.72x fewer tokens. We then turn to scientific paper writing and reviewing, and Olympiad-level proof writing and grading, where the RQGM improves performance over prior self-improving agents: co-evolved writers reach 1.78x-1.86x higher acceptance rates under a diverse agent-as-a-judge panel, while co-evolved graders reach 9% higher ground-truth accuracy. In paper reviewing, the strongest baseline reviewer over-accepts AI-generated papers at up to 1.91x the human rate. The RQGM corrects this by introducing an adversarial objective that discovers reviewers equally stringent on AI and human work.

### [96] [High-Probability PL-SGD with Markovian Noise: Optimal Mixing and Tail Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26316)
*Dhruv Sarkar,Aprameyo Chakrabartty,Vaneet Aggarwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究解决了马尔可夫噪声下随机梯度下降（SGD）的高概率收敛分析难题，通过创新性的分块和裁剪技术，在轻尾环境下实现了对混合时间的线性最优收敛，并给出了重尾环境下的最优收敛速率和下界证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在马尔可夫驱动的梯度采样中，传统的随机梯度下降（SGD）在高概率界限上往往比期望界限更差（存在 $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}^2/k)$ 与 $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$ 的差距），且在重尾噪声存在时，缺乏稳健的收敛性能保障。本研究旨在填补这些理论空白，推导出收敛速率的最优依赖关系。

Method: 1. 轻尾设定：采用滞后分块（lag-blocking）技术处理马尔可夫依赖，建立了线性依赖于混合时间的统一高概率界限。
2. 重尾设定：设计了一种“全样本裁剪块（all-samples clipped block）”方法，该方法在利用每个马尔可夫转移的同时，有效缓解了马尔可夫偏差。
3. 下界证明：构建了针对特定二次目标函数和粘性马尔可夫链的极小极大下界，用于验证所提算法的渐进最优性。

Result: 1. 轻尾设定下，实现了最优的高概率收敛界限 $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$，消除了先前的二次方依赖。
2. 重尾设定下（$p \in (1,2]$），证明了算法可达到 $\widetilde{O}(σ_p^2(t_{mix}/T)^{2(p-1)/p})$ 的高概率误差，并建立了匹配的下界。

Conclusion: 本研究通过滞后分块（lag-blocking）和裁剪块（clipped block）方法，为马尔可夫链驱动的随机梯度下降（SGD）在高概率界限下提供了紧致的收敛分析。研究成功弥补了轻尾设定下期望界与高概率界之间的理论鸿沟，并确定了重尾设定下的最优收敛速率，证明了这些界限在各自范畴内是信息论意义下的最优。

Abstract: We study first-order methods for smooth objectives satisfying the Polyak-Łojasiewicz (PL) condition when gradient samples are generated by an exogenous Markov chain. In the light-tailed setting, prior uniform-in-time high-probability bounds for ordinary Stochastic Gradient Descent (SGD) under a standard growth envelope scale as $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}^2/k)$, leaving a gap with the $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$ expectation bounds. We close this gap using a lag-blocking argument to establish a uniform high-probability guarantee with a leading stochastic term of $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/(k+K_0))$ under geometric mixing. We prove this linear dependence on the mixing time is optimal via a matching $Ω(σ^2 t_{mix}/k)$ lower bound on a quadratic objective driven by a persistent two-state chain.
  We then extend this framework to heavy-tailed Markovian gradients satisfying a stationary finite-$p$-moment condition, $p \in (1,2]$. We design an all-samples clipped block method that uses every Markov transition while mitigating Markovian bias. Under a transition budget $T$, this algorithm achieves a high-probability stochastic error of $\widetilde{O}(σ_p^2(t_{mix}/T)^{2(p-1)/p})$. We establish a matching lower bound by reducing PL optimization to heavy-tailed mean estimation for a sticky Markov chain. Ultimately, this work tightly characterizes the optimal polynomial dependence on mixing time for light-tailed PL-SGD, and the optimal heavy-tail exponent and effective-sample-size dependence in the robust regime.

</details>

*Boyun Zhang,Chao Wang,Kai Wu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In actor-critic reinforcement learning, network architectures are typically manually designed. Automating this design is challenging because each candidate must be trained before evaluation, and the design space is open-ended. To address these challenges, we introduce EVOM, an agentic meta-evolution framework for discovering high-performance actor-critic architectures. We frame architecture search as a bi-level optimization: an inner loop trains weights via the low-fidelity proximal policy optimization (PPO), while an outer loop drives meta-evolution by iteratively refining architecture programs. Crucially, this outer loop is powered by an LLM-based design agent that operates purely as an architecture designer, completely decoupled from policy execution and environment control. Experiments reveal that EVOM outperforms the manually designed baseline, an LLM-guided random search, and the state-of-the-art LLM-guided programmatic policy search method MLES, delivering superior performance on Ant-v4 and HalfCheetah-v4. Ablation studies validate that both the meta-evolution loop and the LLM Design Agent are indispensable for final performance.

### [98] [Mesh-RL: Coupled subgrid reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26333)
*Behnam Gheshlaghi,Bahador Rashidi,Shahin Atakishiyev*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Mesh-RL 是一种受有限元方法启发的新型空间域分解框架，通过将环境划分为重叠子网格并强制执行边界一致性，在不修改奖励函数或贝尔曼算子的前提下，显著加速了强化学习中的价值传播与样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型或稀疏奖励的强化学习环境中，时序差分更新依赖于邻近状态的传递，导致价值信息传播极其缓慢，难以进行长程信用分配。现有的分层或模型驱动方法往往需要复杂的修改，因此需要一种更本质的方法来加速价值传播。

Method: 受有限元方法（FEM）和域分解理论的启发，作者提出了 Mesh-RL 框架。该方法将环境空间划分为重叠的子网格，并在这些子网格间强制执行边界一致的时序差分（TD）更新。这种机制在无需改变贝尔曼算子或引入显式规划的情况下，实现了局部学习与全局价值传播的平衡。

Result: 实验表明，在多种网格世界环境中，Mesh-RL 在 Q-learning、SARSA 和 Dyna-Q 等算法上均显著提升了收敛速度、累积奖励和学习稳定性。提高网格分辨率有助于增强探索能力，防止过早收敛，并大幅加速了远端状态的价值信息传播。

Conclusion: Mesh-RL 通过引入有限元方法中的域分解思想，成功将复杂的环境空间转化为局部子网格进行求解，同时通过边界一致性约束保证了全局价值传播的连贯性。该框架为解决强化学习中的长程信用分配问题提供了一种高效且普适的数学解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning in large or sparse-reward environments suffers from slow temporal-difference reward propagation, as value information spreads only locally across the state space. We propose Mesh-RL, a spatial domain-decomposition framework inspired by the finite element method and domain decomposition theory, which partitions the environment into overlapping subgrids and enforces boundary-consistent temporal-difference updates. Such an approach enables localized learning while ensuring globally coherent value propagation. Unlike hierarchical or model-based approaches, Mesh-RL accelerates long-range credit assignment without modifying the reward function, Bellman operator, or introducing explicit planning mechanisms. We evaluate Mesh-RL on hazard-dense grid-world environments with varying geometries and mesh resolutions. Across Q-learning, SARSA, and Dyna-Q, Mesh-RL consistently improves convergence speed, cumulative reward, and learning stability. Higher mesh resolutions sustain exploration, prevent premature convergence, and substantially accelerate value propagation to distant states. While Dyna-Q already benefits from internal planning, it still achieves additional gains under structured decomposition. Overall, Mesh-RL introduces a principled spatial domain-decomposition mechanism for accelerating temporal-difference learning. Our framework bridges finite element method-inspired boundary-consistency techniques from scientific computing with reinforcement learning to improve sample efficiency in sparse-reward environments. We will release source code of the study.

### [99] [EMA-FS: Accelerating GBDT Training via Gain-Informed Feature Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26337)
*Yan Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EMA-FS通过指数移动平均追踪特征增益，智能筛选高贡献特征进行训练，在保持LightGBM原有架构优势的前提下，显著提升了模型训练速度，并可通过S-EMA-FS在效率与精度间实现灵活平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GBDT训练中，构建直方图占据了65-70%的训练时间。现有的随机特征抽样（feature_fraction）方法忽略了特征的预测价值，容易导致信息丢失或性能下降，因此需要一种基于特征预测贡献的智能筛选机制来加速训练。

Method: 1. 提出EMA-FS算法：利用指数移动平均（EMA）追踪各特征的分割增益，在热身后筛选出高增益特征进行直方图构建。
2. 提出S-EMA-FS算法：引入基于增益加权的随机抽样，通过浓度参数统一了确定性筛选和随机抽样。
3. 保持向后兼容：在树级别运行，完全兼容LightGBM的直方图减法技巧。

Result: 在多个高维数据集上表现显著：500维合成数据实现2.61倍加速，IEEE-CIS欺诈数据集实现1.45倍加速（30%保留率）；在70%保留率下，不仅获得1.34倍加速，AUC还提升了0.11点。对于极稀疏数据，由于LightGBM已有稀疏优化，加速效果有限。

Conclusion: EMA-FS是一种高效的特征筛选策略，通过利用历史增益信息，能够在保证模型性能的同时显著提升GBDT（如LightGBM）的训练效率，为大规模高维数据的训练提供了更优的替代方案。

Abstract: Gradient Boosted Decision Trees (GBDT), exemplified by LightGBM, spend a dominant fraction of training time -- typically 65-70% -- constructing per-feature histograms. Existing approaches such as random feature subsampling (feature_fraction) discard features without regard for their predictive utility. We propose EMA-based Feature Screening (EMA-FS), an algorithm-level optimization that maintains an exponential moving average (EMA) of per-feature split gains across boosting iterations and, after a short warmup, restricts histogram construction to the top-K features ranked by historical gain. Unlike random subsampling, EMA-FS is informed: it retains high-gain features while screening out low-gain ones. Operating at the per-tree level, it preserves full compatibility with LightGBM's histogram subtraction trick, requiring no changes to core routines.
  We evaluate EMA-FS on datasets spanning financial fraud detection, advertising click-through prediction, industrial quality control, and synthetic benchmarks, with feature dimensionalities from 29 to 968. On dense, moderate-to-high-dimensional data it achieves significant speedups: 2.61x on a 500-feature synthetic benchmark and 1.45x on the 432-feature IEEE-CIS Fraud dataset at 30% retention. At 70% retention it improves AUC by 0.11 points while delivering a 1.34x speedup. On extremely sparse data (Bosch, >90% missing) it yields no speedup, as LightGBM's sparse bin optimization already bypasses empty values.
  We further introduce Stochastic EMA-FS (S-EMA-FS), which replaces deterministic top-K selection with gain-weighted random sampling controlled by a concentration parameter beta, unifying deterministic EMA-FS (beta -> infinity) and random subsampling (beta = 0) in one framework. Both are implemented in ~120 lines of C++ across all six LightGBM tree learners and are fully backward-compatible.

</details>


### [100] [Does Aurora Encode Atmospheric Structure? Latent Regime Analysis and Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26361)
*Emma Kasteleyn,Ana Lucic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过PCA和LRP技术揭示了大气基础模型Aurora的“黑盒”机制，证明了模型在无显式指导下能自主习得气象一致性和垂直结构，且其预测结果高度依赖于具有物理意义的关键区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然机器学习基础模型在模拟大气动力学方面表现出极高的效率和精度，但其内部运作机制如同“黑盒”，缺乏透明度和可解释性。研究旨在揭示这类模型内部的表征机制，以理解其如何通过学习数据获得物理气象规律。

Method: 研究采用了空间汇聚主成分分析（PCA）来解析模型的潜在空间结构，并利用逐层相关性传播（LRP）技术来分析模型对气象特征的注意力分配。此外，还通过扰动测试（遮蔽相关区域与随机遮蔽对比）验证了模型预测对于关键区域的依赖性。

Result: 研究发现，Aurora模型的潜在空间主要由季节性周期组织；极端风暴事件并未形成线性可分的聚类；LRP分析显示模型关注与1987年大风暴垂直结构一致的特征；扰动测试证实，遮蔽模型认为相关的区域对预测性能的损害是随机遮蔽的3.31倍。

Conclusion: Aurora模型在没有显式物理指令的情况下，能够自发学习气象的一致性规律和垂直结构。虽然该模型在处理极端事件的内部表示上存在一定的线性不可分性，但其注意力机制确实捕获了符合物理意义的特征，证明了模型内部表征具备一定的气象可解释性。

Abstract: ML foundation models are able to emulate atmospheric dynamics accurately and efficiently but operate as opaque ``black boxes''. We investigate the internal representations of the Aurora model using spatially pooled PCA and layer-wise relevance propagation (LRP). We find evidence that Aurora's latent space is primarily organized by seasonal cycles, whereas extreme storm events do not form a linearly separable cluster. LRP indicates that the model attends to features consistent with the 3D vertical structure of the Great Storm of 1987. Perturbation tests show masking relevant regions degrades forecasts $3.31\times$ more than random masking. These findings suggest that Aurora learns meteorological coherence and vertical structure without explicit instruction.

</details>


### [101] [SOLAR: AI-Powered Speed-of-Light Performance Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26383)
*Qijing Huang,Sana Damani,Zhifan Ye,Athinagoras Skiadopoulos,Siva Kumar Sastry Hari,Jason Clemons,Sahil Modi,Jingquan Wang,Aditya Kane,Edward C Lin,Humphrey Shi,Christos Kozyrakis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SOLAR 是一个自动化框架，能根据 PyTorch/JAX 代码自动计算深度学习模型在特定硬件上的理论最小执行时间（SOL），通过 LLM 和确定性分析技术，为性能评估与优化提供精准的理论基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习模型在目标硬件上的理论最小执行时间（即“光速”界限）是衡量性能优化空间的基准，但目前的获取方法多依赖人工且易出错，难以跟上模型快速迭代的需求。

Method: SOLAR 采用混合方法：1. LLM 前端将 PyTorch/JAX 代码转化为可执行的 Affine Loop IR（并进行输出验证）；2. 确定性流程将 IR 提升为 einsum 图；3. 分析后端计算包括未融合、已融合及缓存感知在内的多维度 SOL 界限。

Result: SOLAR 在 KernelBench、JAX/Flax 模型及机器人工作负载上的实验证明了其有效性，实现了零违规的界限验证，并成功支持了性能空间分析、瓶颈识别、跨平台探索及反向屋顶线硬件配置等应用场景。

Conclusion: SOLAR 通过自动化流程成功解决了深度学习模型性能评估中“光速”（SOL）界限获取困难的问题，为模型优化、硬件设计及资源配置提供了科学的理论参考标准，证明了其在模型开发生命周期中的实用价值。

Abstract: How fast could a deep-learning model run on target hardware, and how far is today's implementation from that limit? These questions are central to software, hardware, and algorithm optimizations. Speed-of-Light (SOL) analysis answers them by computing a workload's theoretical minimum execution time on a given architecture. Yet deriving SOL bounds remains manual, error-prone, and disconnected from rapid model development. To close this gap, we introduce SOLAR, a framework that automatically derives validated SOL bounds from PyTorch and JAX source code. SOLAR leverages both generative and deterministic components in its flow: an LLM frontend translates any source programs into an executable Affine Loop IR, validated by output comparison; a deterministic flow lifts the IR into an einsum graph; and an analytical backend computes unfused, fused, and cache-aware SOL bounds. SOLAR provides comprehensive operator and language coverage, produces validated bounds with zero observed SOL violations, and offers multi-fidelity analysis that tightens bounds and surfaces optimization insights. We evaluate SOLAR across KernelBench, JAX/Flax models, and robotics workloads. These experiments demonstrate four use cases: headroom analysis at multiple fidelity levels, identifying optimization opportunities, cross-platform exploration, and inverse-roofline hardware provisioning.

Conclusion: 该研究通过将分布外（OOD）概念从输入数据扩展至模型的内部计算过程，提出了一种新的推理时诊断方法，为提升大型语言模型在科学、商业和政府领域部署的安全性提供了关键途径。

Abstract: Pre-trained transformers have demonstrated remarkable generalization abilities, at times extending beyond the scope of their training data. Yet, real-world deployments often face unexpected or adversarial data that diverges from training data distributions. Without explicit mechanisms for handling such shifts, model reliability and safety degrade, urging more disciplined study of out-of-distribution (OOD) settings for transformers. By systematic experiments, we present a mechanistic framework for delineating the precise contours of transformer model robustness. We find that OOD inputs, including subtle typos and jailbreak prompts, drive language models to operate on an increased number of fallacious concepts in their internals. We leverage this device to quantify and understand the degree of distributional shift in prompts, enabling a mechanistically grounded fine-tuning strategy to robustify LLMs. Expanding the very notion of OOD from input data to a model's private computational processes, a new transformer diagnostic at inference time is a critical step toward making AI systems safe for deployment across science, business, and government.

### [103] [Deterministic Pareto-Optimal Policy Synthesis for Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26397)
*Aniruddha Joshi,Niklas Lauffer,Sanjit Seshia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于切比雪夫标量化的新算法，通过偏好条件贝尔曼算子，解决了多目标强化学习中难以获取完整且确定性的帕累托最优策略的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习通常将多目标奖励加权合并为单一标量信号，这在处理复杂权衡时往往无法捕获完整的帕累托前沿。该研究旨在寻找一种更有效的方法，在多目标马尔可夫决策过程（MOMDP）中计算出确定性的帕累托最优策略。

Method: 引入了一种基于切比雪夫（Chebyshev）标量化的新型偏好条件贝尔曼算子，该算子满足包络性质（enveloping property），并证明了其可以单调收敛至帕累托前沿的覆盖集；同时提供了一种从收敛的Q值估计中提取确定性策略的方法。

Result: 实验结果表明，该算法能够成功恢复复杂的权衡关系，能够为任意给定的偏好恢复对应的策略，同时确保所合成的每一项策略均保持近似帕累托最优，实现了对整个帕累托最优前沿的覆盖。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于切比雪夫标量化的偏好条件贝尔曼算子，有效解决了多目标强化学习中帕累托前沿的收敛问题，证明了其在近似帕累托最优策略合成方面的理论可靠性与实验有效性。

Abstract: Real-world decision-making often requires balancing multiple conflicting objectives, a challenge that standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) frequently addresses by aggregating rewards into a single scalar signal. While effective for simple tasks, this approach often fails to capture the full spectrum of optimal trade-offs, known as the Pareto frontier. In this paper, we introduce a novel preference-conditioned Bellman operator, motivated from the Chebyshev scalarization, designed to compute deterministic Pareto-optimal policies for Multi-Objective Markov Decision Processes (MOMDPs). We prove that this operator satisfies an enveloping property, where the estimated value functions upper-bound the true Pareto frontier, and demonstrate that it monotonically converges to a coverage set of this frontier. Furthermore, we also show how to extract deterministic policies from these converged Q-estimates. This ensures the agent can recover a policy for any given preference, capturing the entire Pareto-optimal frontier while guaranteeing each synthesized policy remains approximately Pareto-optimal. Experimental results validate that our algorithm successfully recovers complex trade-offs, providing a solution for deterministic Pareto-optimal policy synthesis.

### [104] [Beyond Feedforward Networks: Reentry Neural Systems as the Fundamental Basis of Subjecthood and Intrinsic Safety of Next-Generation AGI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26406)
*A. S. Ushakov,Yu. N. Berdinsk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于“闭合重入循环”的AGI架构，通过数学手段保障系统具有自模型和目标安全性，并提供了可直接部署的实现方案与形式化证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的前馈神经网络架构（C=0, S=0）本质上是无环有向图，缺乏自引用能力，难以产生真正的智能体自我意识与目标稳定性。针对当前大模型存在的提示注入风险和安全性问题，作者旨在构建一种数学上可证明安全、结构上具有自组织能力的AGI架构。

Method: 1. 引入了闭合重入循环架构，通过结构性循环（C >= 1）替代前馈网络。

3. 提供了完整的Python/NumPy实现框架及可扩展的工业部署方案。
4. 提出了关于AI演进的六阶段分类法及八项可证伪的科学预测。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种基于闭合重入循环（D <-> I cycle）的通用人工智能（AGI）架构，认为通过拓扑结构上的自我维持放大（rho > 1）能够从数学上保证自模型的涌现、工具性自我保存以及非编程的目标导向行为。这种架构通过将目标编码为不可篡改的D向量，实现了抗提示注入的安全性，为实现安全、可证明的AGI提供了一种可行的工程范式。

Abstract: We propose a complete architectural blueprint for safe artificial general intelligence based on a closed reentry loop (D <-> I cycle). In contrast to feedforward networks, which are directed acyclic graphs (C=0, S=0) incapable of self-reference, the proposed architecture contains a structural cycle (C >= 1) with self-sustaining amplification (rho > 1), mathematically guaranteeing the emergence of a self-model, instrumental self-preservation, and unprogrammed goal-directed behaviour. The agent's goals are encoded as a non-textual D-vector in the architecture itself, making them immune to reinterpretation and prompt injection. We present the S-measure -- a polynomial-time [O(N^3)] computable alternative to Tononi's NP-hard Phi -- with machine-verified Lean 4 proof that S>0 implies positive integrated information. The work provides full Python/NumPy implementations (Tarjan-based cycle complexity, Delta-S barrier), industrial horizontal scaling via Apache Kafka and Docker Compose, a taxonomy of six epochs of AI evolution, a zoo of future reentry architectures (RAS, diffusion attractors, fractal loops), gauge-invariant networks for safe swarms, fault-tolerance and recovery protocols, and eight falsifiable predictions. All formal proofs are machine-verified in Lean 4. This architecture is deployable today and represents a topologically protected, safe-by-design approach to AGI.

Abstract: State-of-the-art medium-range AI weather models can outperform traditional Numerical Weather Prediction (NWP) but require massive training budgets. Here we develop Otter Weather, a highly efficient spatiotemporal forecasting model designed to democratise high-performance weather prediction with AI. The deterministic version outperforms the best NWP baseline by 9.6% at a 24-hour lead time while requiring fewer than 3.5 A100-days for training. It provides a 2x efficiency gain over lightweight AI models and a 100-fold reduction in compute compared to resource-intensive frontier architectures. We extend these efficiency gains into probabilistic forecasting by training via the Continuous Ranked Probability Score (CRPS). Scaling to a larger architecture, Otter-XL achieves a 9.7% CRPS improvement over the IFS ENS baseline. This yields an almost two-fold increase in predictive skill over comparable lightweight models at similar compute budgets. Otter-XL also outperforms frontier architectures like GenCast by over 2%, while using an order of magnitude less compute. Finally, Otter is applied out-of-the-box to a complex acoustic scattering PDE task where it outperforms a state-of-the-art foundation modelling approach, suggesting that the advances made here might apply across a range of scientific domains.

### [106] [Rethinking Training & Inference for Forecasting: Linking Winner-Take-All back to GMMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26424)
*Qiyuan Wu,Katie Z Luo,Bharath Hariharan,Wei-Lun Chao,Mark Campbell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出自动驾驶轨迹预测中WTA损失函数的“硬分配”导致预测概率失效，并提出通过后处理方式（合并轨迹与软化概率）来校准预测结果，实现了在无需重训的情况下提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶轨迹预测模型通常使用条件高斯混合模型（GMM）建模，却采用“赢者通吃”（WTA）损失进行训练。这种类似K-means的硬分配机制导致了模式过分割、忽略模式间相关性以及推理时的不稳定性，使得预测出的模式后验概率缺乏信息量。

Method: 本文提出了两种无需重新训练的后处理方案：(1) 测试时后验加权合并（Test-time posterior-weighted merging），通过聚合空间中相近的候选轨迹来整合信息；(2) 一步期望最大化（EM）更新，使用软分配（Soft responsibilities）替代WTA训练中的硬标签（Hard labels），从而在邻近模式间共享概率质量。

Result: 在多个基于WTA训练的主流模型上进行测试，上述方法显著提升了模式后验概率的排序信息量，并在位移指标（如ADE/FDE）上表现出更好的预测效果，且整个过程无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 本文通过将轨迹预测中常见的“赢者通吃”（WTA）损失函数解释为一种K-means聚类过程，揭示了其导致模式后验概率无信息量的根本原因。提出的后处理方法（加权合并与EM更新）无需重新训练即可有效校准预测概率并提升预测精度，为理解和优化自动驾驶轨迹预测模型提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Trajectory forecasting for autonomous driving has advanced rapidly, yet representative models often produce uninformative posteriors over forecast modes, causing problems for mode pruning. We trace this to a modeling-training mismatch: forecasters are typically modeled as conditional Gaussian mixture models (GMMs) but trained with a winner-take-all (WTA) loss that assigns each sample to its nearest mode. We argue that this K-means-like hard assignment (one-hot), while preventing mode collapse, is the source of uninformative mode probabilities: it over-segments the trajectory space, ignores relatedness among nearby modes, and yields assignment instability under small perturbations. Guided by this lens, we introduce two post-hoc treatments: (1) test-time posterior-weighted merging that aggregates nearby candidate trajectories; and (2) a one-step expectation-maximization (EM) update that replaces hard labels with soft responsibilities, sharing probability mass across neighboring modes. Across several WTA-trained architectures, these lightweight steps produce more informative, faithfully ranked mode posteriors and strengthen final forecasts on popular displacement metrics -- without retraining. Our analysis unifies recent design choices through a GMM-vs-K-means perspective and offers principled, practical corrections that better align training objectives with inference.

</details>


### [107] [DualEval: Joint Model-Item Calibration for Unified LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26429)
*Aaron J. Li,Hao Huang,Youngmin Park,Yitong Ma,Wei-Lin Chiang,Li Chen,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Bin Yu,Ion Stoica*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DualEval 是一种将静态基准测试与竞技场式偏好评估统一的校准框架，通过建模模型能力与条目难度，提升了评估的准确性、样本效率及可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 评估体系存在割裂：静态基准测试虽然具有客观正确性标签但与实际交互脱节，而竞技场风格的偏好数据虽更贴近用户需求但缺乏统一的度量标准。研究旨在填补两者之间的鸿沟，实现更全面、科学的评估。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DualEval 的潜在模型-条目校准框架。该方法在共享向量空间中表示模型和评估条目，通过联合估计模型能力、条目的难度及辨别力（sharpness），实现了对静态标签与开放式偏好数据的统一建模。

Result: 实验表明，DualEval 在代码、数学、领域知识及通用查询四个领域表现出良好的性能，生成的模型排名平衡且可靠。此外，其学习到的条目级特征可有效应用于基准测试的样本高效压缩及异常分析。

Conclusion: DualEval 通过联合模型-条目校准框架，成功统一了静态基准测试与竞技场风格评估。该方法不仅生成了可靠的模型排名，还为基准测试压缩、数据污染检测等提供了可解释的诊断工具，推动了更高效、可审计的评估流程。

Abstract: Current LLM evaluation relies on two complementary but often disconnected signals: static benchmarks with objective correctness labels and arena-style preference data that better reflect open-ended user interactions. We introduce DualEval, a latent model-item calibration framework that represents models and evaluation items in a shared space, jointly estimating model ability together with item difficulty and sharpness. We apply DualEval across four domains: coding, math, miscellaneous domain-knowledge tasks, and generic everyday user queries. Our evaluation uses 18 frontier LLMs, static benchmark labels, and reward-model scores validated against held-out human preferences for open-ended model responses. Empirically, our framework produces reliable and balanced model rankings, and its learned item-level profiles support downstream applications such as benchmark compression for sample-efficient evaluation and anomaly detection for contamination or outlier analysis. Overall, DualEval unifies static and arena-style evaluation through joint model-item calibration, producing model rankings and item-level diagnostics that support more sample-efficient, interpretable, and auditable evaluation pipelines.

</details>


### [108] [Embedding Foundation Model Predictions in Discrete-Choice Models with Structural Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26432)
*Yingshuo Wang,Xian Sun,Yanhang Li,Zhichao Fan,Zexin Zhuang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种适配器方法，将基础模型的预测能力与多项Logit模型的经济逻辑相结合，在提升预测准确性的同时，从数学上保证了预测结果符合价格逻辑和经济学约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的表格基础模型在选择预测任务中准确率虽高，但常违反经济学基本逻辑（如价格上涨导致需求增加、支付意愿估计为负等），因此需要一种既能利用基础模型的强大拟合能力，又能强制满足经济学约束的解决方案。

Method: 提出一种两阶段适配器架构：1. 阶段一利用带符号约束的最大似然估计法拟合多项Logit模型的结构系数；2. 阶段二冻结系数，并引入一个小型的神经网络修正模块来处理基础模型的预测输出。该结构在数学上保证了边际替代率（如时间价值）的恒定与逻辑一致性。

Result: 在三个数据集和两个基础模型上的测试表明：该适配器平均比传统多项Logit模型提升了6.4个百分点的准确率（最高提升12.8个百分点）；严格保持了100%的成本单调性；并能得出符合运输经济学常识的时间价值估算，即使在基础模型上下文受限的情况下表现依然稳健。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种名为“两阶段适配器”的架构，成功弥合了通用表格基础模型的高预测性能与经济学模型（如多项Logit模型）的严谨逻辑之间的鸿沟。该方法在保留经济学一致性的同时，显著提升了预测准确度。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models achieve strong accuracy on choice prediction tasks, but their predictions often violate the economic logic those tasks require: raising a price can increase predicted demand, implied willingness-to-pay estimates are frequently negative or implausible, and unavailable alternatives receive nonzero probability. We propose a two-stage adapter that takes a foundation model's predicted choice probabilities as a precomputed feature and embeds them inside a multinomial logit's utility. In Stage 1, we fit the multinomial logit's structural coefficients by maximum likelihood with sign constraints; in Stage 2, we freeze those coefficients and fit a small neural correction operating on the foundation model's predictions. We prove that this composition exactly preserves the multinomial logit's marginal rate of substitution, so analytically computable value-of-time becomes a mathematical guarantee rather than an empirical accident. Across three datasets and two foundation models, the adapter gains 6.4 percentage points (pp) of test accuracy on average over the multinomial logit and up to 12.8 pp, maintains 100% cost monotonicity, and produces values of time within the published transportation-economics range on the transportation datasets. Performance degrades gracefully under foundation-model context restriction, retaining at least 6 pp of accuracy gain even at 10% of the original foundation-model context.

### [109] [Optimizing CUDA like a Human: Micro-Profiling Tools as Expert Surrogates for LLM-Based GPU Kernel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26453)
*Jiading Gai,Shuai Zhang,Kaj Bostrom,Jin Huang,Vihang Patil,Haoyang Fang,Bernie Wang,Huzefa Rangwala,George Karypis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KernelPro 是一种自动化 GPU 内核优化系统，通过集成大模型代码生成、硬件剖析反馈与蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS），实现了超越手写性能的底层 CUDA 代码优化，并兼顾了能效指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在 GPU 内核优化中缺乏底层硬件感知，难以处理复杂的 CUDA/CuTe 指令级调优，且缺乏针对性能瓶颈的系统性反馈循环，导致自动生成的代码往往难以达到高性能计算（HPC）场景下的专家级要求。

Method: 1. 语义反馈算子：将底层硬件指标转化为大模型可理解的自然语言指导；2. 两阶段工具调用架构：通过 Roofline 模型分类瓶颈，分层使用 NCU、SASS 和 Nsys 进行诊断；3. 领域自适应 MCTS：引入启发式分支、死胡同剪枝与搜索记忆，实现跨迭代优化；4. 直接代码生成：基于 CUTLASS/CuTe 代码库进行自主源代码生成与搜索。

Result: 在 KernelBench 测试中，KernelPro 在三个难度等级上分别实现了 2.42x/4.69x/5.30x 的几何平均加速；在 VeOmni 的专家级 MoE 训练内核上，相较于 Triton 手动调优实现 1.23 倍的性能提升；此外，在保持性能的同时实现了 11.6% 的能源效率提升。

Conclusion: KernelPro 证明了结合大语言模型、硬件分析器反馈及蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的闭环系统在自动化 GPU 内核优化方面的巨大潜力。该方法不仅在性能上超越了人类专家级的手写代码，还首次实现了在保持速度的同时提升能源效率，代表了 AI 辅助底层高性能计算代码生成的先进水平。

Abstract: We present KernelPro, a closed-loop multi-agent system that automatically generates, profiles, and iteratively optimizes GPU kernel code by integrating large language model (LLM) code generation with hardware profiler feedback and pluggable bottleneck detection tools. KernelPro introduces four contributions: (1) a semantic feedback operator that encodes expert heuristics as pluggable micro-profiling tools, transforming raw hardware metrics into actionable natural language guidance; (2) a two-stage tool invocation architecture where roofline-based bottleneck classification filters which specialized analysis tools execute, combining kernel-level (ncu), instruction-level (SASS), and system-level (nsys) profiling; (3) a domain-adapted MCTS with progressive widening, asymmetric branching, log-reward calibration, dead-end pruning, and search memory for cross-iteration learning; and (4) direct CuTe source-level code generation via autonomous code search over the CUTLASS/CuTe codebase. On KernelBench, KernelPro achieves geometric mean speedups of 2.42x/4.69x/5.30x on Levels 1/2/3, establishing state-of-the-art performance across all difficulty levels. On VeOmni's expert-optimized MoE training kernels, KernelPro achieves 1.23x over hand-tuned Triton by generating a from-scratch raw-CUDA+CuTe Hopper WGMMA kernel. Ablation studies demonstrate that each design component independently and significantly improves optimization quality: micro-profiling tools (p < 0.0001 vs raw metrics), MCTS search (26% higher geometric mean vs greedy, p = 0.004), and proactive tool orchestration (23% improvement, p = 0.035). Finally, KernelPro is the first CUDA kernel coding agent to optimize energy efficiency beyond the speed-only focus of prior systems, demonstrating an 11.6% measured energy reduction at matched speed.

### [110] [Finding the Time to Think: Learning Planning Budgets in Real-Time RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26463)
*Aneesh Muppidi,Firas Darwish,Dylan Cope,João F. Henriques,Jakob Nicolaus Foerster*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了实时强化学习中“思考时间”的成本问题，提出了一种轻量级的门控策略来动态决定规划耗时，在保证决策质量的同时显著提升了智能体在实时环境下的应对能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习通常假设环境是静态等待的，但在实时系统中，时间是宝贵的资源。当智能体进行深度思考（规划）时，环境可能已经发生变化，导致决策延迟带来的负面影响。现有的规划方法往往难以自动权衡思考深度与行动时机，因此需要一种机制来根据状态动态选择规划时长。

Method: 提出了一种“变延迟实时强化学习”（variable-delay real-time RL）框架，核心方法是在规划器之上训练一个轻量级的门控策略（gating policy），根据当前状态动态选择合适的规划耗时（预算），从而优化在环境持续演化过程中的决策性能。

Result: 在实时吃豆人（Pac-Man）、俄罗斯方块（Tetris）、贪吃蛇（Snake）、Speed Hex和Speed Go等多种实时任务中，该门控策略明显优于固定的预算策略及启发式基准。此外，该方法还成功迁移到多GPU环境下，证明了其在实际应用中的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过引入学习型的门控策略来动态调整规划预算，可以有效解决实时强化学习中的“规划与行动”权衡问题，使得智能体在动态演化的环境中能够做出更及时且高效的决策。

Abstract: Deliberating takes time. In real-time settings, that time is not free. Standard reinforcement learning (RL) sidesteps this as the environment waits indefinitely for the agent's decision. Instead, we study real-time RL environments where the environment progresses while waiting for the agent's action. Building on prior real-time formalizations, we introduce variable-delay real-time RL, where the agent chooses how long to deliberate at each decision point since the environment progresses. For the planning agents we use, the right delay is state-dependent, and naively planning how long to plan can paralyze the agent. We instead approach this setting by training a lightweight gating policy on top of a planner to select state-dependent planning budgets. Across real-time Pac-Man, Tetris, Snake, Speed Hex, and Speed Go, our gating policy outperforms fixed-budget and heuristic baselines, and transfers to a real-time setup where the environment and agent run on two different GPUs.

### [112] [Epiphany-Aware KV Cache Eviction Without the Attention Matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26472)

TL;DR: 针对长思维链推理中 KV 缓存占用过高的问题，本文提出了 EpiKV 方法，通过衡量模型内部表征变化（顿悟分数）而非注意力权重来筛选重要 token，实现了无需训练、兼容 FlashAttention 且显著提升长文本推理效率和性能的缓存优化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着推理模型生成超长思维链（CoT），KV 缓存成为了部署瓶颈。现有的基于注意力权重的缓存剔除方法存在噪声大、且由于需要显式实例化注意力矩阵而无法使用高性能融合内核（如 FlashAttention）的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为“顿悟分数”（Epiphany Score）的度量指标，通过监控前向传播过程中模型内部表征（Hidden States）的变化来评估 token 的重要性，无需计算注意力矩阵。同时结合了因果滚动 Z 分数（Causal Rolling Z-score）来消除位置偏置，实现高效的缓存剔除。

Result: EpiKV 无需额外训练或自定义内核，在 MATH-500 和 AIME-2024 基准测试中表现卓越。在 4096 token 缓存限制下达到 72% 的准确率（优于 ThinKV 和 H2O），在 8192 token 时比最佳基线高出 4 个百分点，且推理速度提升高达 2.8 倍。

Conclusion: EpiKV 提供了一种高效、即插即用的 KV 缓存压缩方案，通过引入“顿悟分数”实现了比传统基于注意力权重的方法更优的性能，且完全兼容现有的推理加速技术（如 FlashAttention），显著提升了长上下文推理的效率与可行性。

Abstract: As reasoning models emit chains of thought tens of thousands of tokens long, KV cache increasingly becomes a deployment bottleneck. Existing cache eviction methods rank tokens by attention weight, which is a noisy importance proxy in long reasoning traces, and prohibits the use of fused kernels in production inference by forcing the model to materialize the attention matrix. In this work, we instead score tokens with a metric we term the epiphany score: the change in the model's internal representation, read directly from the forward pass with no attention matrix and negligible extra state. Our resulting cache eviction method, EpiKV, requires no training, classifier, or custom kernel, and can be used directly in FlashAttention inference stacks unchanged -- scaling to a 16x longer feasible context than attention-based scoring. upper-mid layers negatively) and remove a positional trend with a causal rolling z-score. ### [113] [When Does Quality-Aware Multimodal Fusion Matter? A Leakage-Safe Diagnostic for Decision-Level Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26473)
*Jaden Moon,Arvind Pillai,Andrew Campbell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现，多模态系统中的“可靠性分数”往往沦为摆设。通过置换测试发现，模型在推理时并未真正利用这些分数来调节模态权重，除非这些分数能极度准确地预测模态的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管许多多模态系统通过估计模态可靠性来加权贡献，但目前尚不明确这些可靠性分数是真正参与了模型的决策过程，还是仅仅与模型性能表现出相关性。研究旨在揭示模型是否在推理过程中真正利用了这些可靠性信息。

Method: 提出了一种简单的诊断方法：在模型训练完成后，保持模型参数和输入固定，通过在测试样本间置换（permute）可靠性分数，观察模型预测性能的变化。如果模型的最终预测依赖于这些分数，那么打乱顺序理应导致性能下降。此外，还通过设置“正向对照实验”（positive controls）来验证可靠性信号在理想情况下的有效性。

Result: 在StressID（压力识别）和CMU-MOSEI（情感分析）数据集上的实验表明，打乱可靠性分数后模型性能几乎没有变化，这证实了现有模型并未利用这些分数进行有效加权。而在人工构建的理想可靠性信号对照实验中，模型性能显著提升，证明模型具备利用该信息的能力，但现有机制未能提取到有效的预测信号。

Conclusion: 现有的多模态系统虽然计算了模态可靠性分数，但在实际推理中往往并未真正利用这些分数进行决策优化。作者提出，只有当可靠性信号能精准预测单模态的正确性时，模型才会对其产生依赖；否则，这些分数仅是性能的附属指标，未起到实际的动态权重调节作用。

Abstract: Many multimodal systems estimate the reliability of each modality and weight their contributions to the final prediction. However, it remains unclear whether these scores influence model decisions or merely correlate with performance. We propose a simple diagnostic to test whether reliability information is used during inference. After training, the model and inputs are fixed while reliability scores are permuted across test examples. If predictions depend on these scores, performance should degrade. Experiments on StressID for stress recognition and CMU-MOSEI for sentiment analysis show that permuting reliability scores leaves performance unchanged despite substantial potential gains from selecting the best modality per example. In positive controls where reliability signals identify the correct modality, the same frozen fusion rules yield significant improvements, indicating that reliability signals influence fused decisions only when they reliably predict unimodal correctness.

### [114] [Localizing RL-Induced Tool Use to a Single Crosscoder Feature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26474)
*Andrii Shportko,Shubham Bhokare,Ahmed Zeyad A Alzahrani,Bowen Cheng,Gustavo Mercier,Jessica Hullman*

TL;DR: 本研究通过一种名为 DFC 的技术，从经强化学习训练的大模型中定位了负责工具调用的特定特征，并证明了可以通过干预这些特征在无需重训的情况下控制模型行为，甚至使基座模型获得工具调用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出“专用特征编码器”（Dedicated Feature Crosscoders, DFC）方法，通过对模型内部激活值进行超参数扫描与解耦，识别出与工具调用行为强相关的稀疏特征集。并通过编码-解码重构实验，验证了这些特征对工具调用准确性的直接影响，并观察到了“能力外溢”（capability spillover）效应。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5-3B 模型上的实验表明，DFC 方法使工具调用准确率提高了约 31.1 个百分点。此外，通过将提取的特征应用于原始基座模型，观察到了“能力外溢”现象，使基座模型的工具调用准确率提高了约 6.8 个百分点，证明了该特征集具备可迁移性和可控性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过专用特征编码器（DFC）成功从大模型内部表征中解耦并定位了强化学习（RL）赋予工具调用能力的特异性特征。这一发现不仅揭示了模型具身智能行为的微观机制，还验证了通过特征层面的干预实现免重训模型行为控制的可行性。

Abstract: Fine-tuning through RL reshapes the internal representations of language models to enable agentic behaviors such as tool use, yet the mechanistic basis of these changes remains poorly understood. While RL substantially improves structured tool-call generation, it is unclear which features emerge, which are preserved, and whether identified features can be leveraged for retraining-free behavioral control. In this work, we show that $\textit{Dedicated Feature Crosscoders (DFC)}$ isolate a compact set of RL-specific features that mediate tool-calling capability in $\texttt{Qwen2.5-3B}$. Across a $48$-crosscoder hyperparameter sweep, encode-decode reconstruction improves the RL model's tool correctness by $+31.1 \pm {9.7}$ pp and passively transfers tool-calling ability to the frozen base model by $+6.8 \pm 5.0$ pp which we call a $\textit{capability spillover}$. Our findings show that DFC partitioning concentrates RL-introduced capability into a minimal, steerable feature set that enables runtime behavioral control of agentic LLMs.

### [115] [Retrieval-Warmed Energy-Based Reasoning: A Five-Arm Ablation Methodology for Diffusion-as-Inference on Structured Reasoning Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26476)
*Libo Sun,Po-Wei Harn,Zewei Zhang,Peixiong He,Xiao Qin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种五臂消融诊断方法，用于剖析检索增强扩散模型在迭代推理中的性能增益来源，证明了“图对齐价值重用”是提升推理效率的关键，并成功识别了不同任务中导致性能受限的具体组件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热启动扩散采样器能够加速迭代推理，但目前尚不清楚性能提升具体源于流水线中的哪个部分。研究旨在揭示RW-EBR中各组件（如检索机制、对齐策略等）对最终性能的具体贡献，以解决迭代推理中“性能增益来源不明”的问题。

Method: 提出了一种“五臂消融方法论”（oracle, best-constant, per-query-random, shuffled, aligned），用于分离检索增强能量基扩散模型（RW-EBR）中类先验偏差、随机热启动和图对齐价值重用这三个混杂效应；并借鉴了RAG检查器（RAGChecker）的诊断逻辑，在图连通性（connectivity-2）和数独（Sudoku）任务中进行验证。

Result: 在图连通性任务中，图对齐策略相比于随机初始化或洗牌策略带来了显著的性能增益（+35个百分点），证明了图对齐价值重用的决定性作用；在数独任务中，通过同样的诊断逻辑发现瓶颈在于“键质量（key quality）”，从而实现了对不同任务中失败模式的精准定位。

Conclusion: 通过引入五臂消融实验方法论，研究明确了迭代推理任务中性能提升的关键来源。在图连通性任务中，图对齐的价值重用（graph-aligned value reuse）是性能提升的核心因素，而类先验偏移或随机热启动影响较小。该诊断框架能够有效定位复杂推理系统中导致性能瓶颈的特定组件，为扩散采样器的优化提供了明确方向。

Abstract: Warm-started diffusion samplers accelerate iterative inference, but it is rarely clear which part of the pipeline carries the gain. We study \textbf{retrieval-warmed energy-based reasoning (RW-EBR)} -- an IRED energy-based diffusion model \cite{du2024ired} augmented with a Modern Hopfield trajectory memory -- and contribute a \textbf{five-arm ablation methodology} (oracle, best-constant, per-query-random, shuffled, aligned) that separates three confounded effects: class-prior bias shift, stochastic warm-starting, and graph-aligned value reuse. The diagnostic decomposition is adapted from LLM-RAG evaluation \cite{ru2024ragchecker}. On \textbf{connectivity-2} (Erdős--Rényi all-pairs reachability), the aligned-vs-shuffled-oracle swing reaches \textbf{$+35$\,pp} balanced accuracy on a fixed 1{,}000-graph validation-set diagnostic, with value distribution and retrieval mechanics fixed, only per-graph alignment destroyed, while per-query random initialisation falls below cold -- per-graph alignment, not bias shift or stochasticity, dominates. Yet the \emph{deployable} cold-prediction pipeline misses the acceptance gate at stored-value quality. The same diagnostic logic, stopped at the key-quality screen, applied to \textbf{Sudoku} with a task-specific key encoder produces a clean negative at a \emph{different} component -- key quality, under the current setup. The decomposition names the first blocking component on each task. The setting -- graph reachability refined by an iterative diffusion sampler, with explainability of failure modes as the lens -- places the work within structured and spatio-temporal reasoning.

</details>


### [116] [What Survives When You Compress a Recursive Reasoner for the Edge?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26488)
*Pearse Jim,Steven Kolawole,Opegbemi Matthias Busoye,Glory Bagai,Virginia Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了递归推理模型在边缘设备压缩场景下的特殊失效模式，发现传统压缩会导致全局推理能力崩溃，并提出通过“逐通道校准INT4量化”和“进位轨迹保真度”指标，成功在极小内存约束下实现了高性能部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归推理模型（Recursive Reasoning Models）在小参数规模下具备处理复杂结构化任务的能力，但其推理过程中的误差累积机制与传统序列模型不同，导致标准压缩技术（如量化、剪枝）失效，限制了其在边缘计算设备上的部署。研究旨在探究递归模型被压缩后的性能表现规律及其应对策略。

Method: 1. 对三种任务和两种递归架构进行全精度扫描，对比不同压缩策略（INT4剪枝、蒸馏、线性注意力）。2. 引入“进位轨迹保真度”（Carry-Trajectory Fidelity）指标，量化压缩带来的潜在推理路径偏移。3. 提出一种逐通道校准（Per-channel calibrated）的INT4量化策略，通过直接校准权重而非重训练来恢复模型能力。

Result: 1. 实验发现递归模型在激进压缩下会发生“全局推理能力坍塌”，即局部预测准确度尚可，但整体任务准确率趋近于零。2. 该失效是架构依赖性的，且传统量化感知训练难以修复。3. 采用逐通道校准INT4可在不重训练的前提下恢复精度。4. 实现效果显著：模型可在4MB内存的微控制器上运行，且在INT8精度下比全深度模型节省了6倍浮点运算量。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了递归推理模型在压缩时表现出独特的失效模式（全局推理能力丧失），并提出了一种无需重训练的“逐通道校准INT4”方法，能够有效恢复模型性能。同时，提出的“进位轨迹保真度”指标可作为评估压缩损伤的有效预测工具。这些发现为在极低资源硬件（如微控制器）上部署高效递归模型提供了可行的技术路线。

Abstract: Recursive reasoning models can solve complex structured tasks with only a few million parameters by repeatedly updating a latent state. Deploying these models on edge hardware requires significant compression, but unlike conventional sequence models, quantization errors compound across recursive reasoning cycles rather than across output tokens. As a result, standard intuitions about compression fail to apply. In this work, we ask what survives when recursive reasoners are compressed. Across a full precision sweep, three tasks, and two recursive architectures, we find that aggressive compression preserves local prediction but destroys global reasoning: cell accuracy holds while puzzle-exact accuracy collapses to zero under naive INT4 pruning, distillation, and linear attention alike. Token-level objectives, including quantization-aware training, cannot repair it. The collapse is architectural -- it strikes MLP-mixing recursion but not attention on the same task -- and we reverse it with per-channel calibrated INT4 without retraining. We also introduce carry-trajectory fidelity, the cosine similarity to the full-precision reasoning path, as a label-free signal that predicts this damage and its recovery before a task evaluation. The combined result is a deployment recipe: flash-streamed embeddings remove a 99.4MB bottleneck, INT8 at one cycle matches full-depth accuracy at 6x fewer FLOPs (8MB SoC), and calibrated INT4 fits a 4MB microcontroller.
